Having proved a preservation property in the last chapter, a natural
next step would be to prove progress. That is, to prove a property
of the form

    If Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v, then either M is a lambda abstraction or M â€”â†’ N for some N.

Such a property would tell us that having a denotation implies either
reduction to normal form or divergence. This is indeed true, but we
can prove a much stronger property! In fact, having a denotation that
is a function value (not `âŠ¥`) implies reduction to a lambda
abstraction (no divergence).

This stronger property, reformulated a bit, is known as _adequacy_.
That is, if a term `M` is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then `M` reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    â„° M â‰ƒ â„° (Æ› N)  implies M â€”â†  Æ› N' for some N'

Recall that `â„° M â‰ƒ â„° (Æ› N)` is equivalent to saying that
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` for some `v` and `w`. We will show that
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` implies reduction a lambda abstraction.

It is well known that a term can reduce to a lambda abstraction using
full Î² reduction if and only if it can reduce to a lambda abstraction
using the call-by-name reduction strategy. So we shall prove that
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` implies that `M` halts under call-by-name evaluation,
which we define with a big-step semantics written `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c`, where
`c` is a closure (a term paired with an environment) and `Î³'` is an
environment that maps variables to closures

So we will show that `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` implies `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c`,
provided `Î³` and `Î³'` are appropriate related.  The proof will
be an induction on the derivation of `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, and to
strengthen the induction hypothesis, we will relate semantic values to
closures using a _logical relation_ `ğ•`.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* We loosen the requirement that `M` result in a function value and
  instead require that `M` result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the call-by-name big-step semantics of the lambda calculus
  and prove that it is deterministic.

* We define the logical relation `ğ•` that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms `ğ”¼` and environments `ğ”¾`.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'` and `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, then `ğ”¼ v (clos M Î³')`.

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.


## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

If a value `u` is greater than a function, then an even greater value `u'`
is too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun-âŠ‘"></a><a id="3831" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3831" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ‘</a> <a id="3842" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3844" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="3846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3846" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="3848" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3848" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="3851" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="3858" class="Symbol">}</a>

The bottom value `âŠ¥` is not greater than a function.

If the join of two values `u` and `u'` is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

On the other hand, if neither of `u` and `u'` is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-âŠ”"></a><a id="4910" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4910" class="Function">not-AboveFun-âŠ”</a> <a id="4925" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4927" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="4929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4929" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4931" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4931" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="4934" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4941" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="4958" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="4960" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="4962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3646" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4929" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4973" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="4975" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="4977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3646" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4986" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4931" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
               <a id="5004" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="5006" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="5008" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3646" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5017" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4929" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŠ”</a> <a id="5022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4931" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5024" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4910" class="Function">not-AboveFun-âŠ”</a> <a id="5041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5041" class="Bound">naf1</a> <a id="5046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5046" class="Bound">naf2</a> <a id="5051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5051" class="Bound">af12</a>
    <a id="5060" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="5065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4397" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ”</a> <a id="5076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5051" class="Bound">af12</a>
<a id="5081" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5085" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5087" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚</a> <a id="5092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5092" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5096" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5098" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5092" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5116" class="Bound">naf1</a>
<a id="5121" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5125" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5127" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚‚</a> <a id="5132" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5132" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5136" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5138" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5152" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5132" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5156" class="Bound">naf2</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-âŠ”-inv"></a><a id="5303" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5303" class="Function">not-AboveFun-âŠ”-inv</a> <a id="5322" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5324" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="5326" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5326" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5328" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5328" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5340" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="5342" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="5344" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3646" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5353" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5354" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5326" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŠ”</a> <a id="5358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5328" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5360" class="Symbol">)</a>

The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

## Big-step semantics for call-by-name lambda calculus

To better align with the denotational semantics, we shall use an
environment-passing big-step semantics. Because this is call-by-name,
an environment maps each variable to a closure, that is, to a term
paired with its environment. (Environments and closures are mutually
recursive.) We define environments and closures as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ClosEnv"></a><a id="6664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2980" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="6682" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6684" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

<a id="6689" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Clos"></a><a id="6694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="6699" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6701" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6705" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Clos.clos"></a><a id="6713" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6713" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="6718" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6720" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="6722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6722" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="6723" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6725" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6727" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6728" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6730" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6722" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6734" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="6736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="6737" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6739" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6722" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6751" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6753" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a>

<a id="6759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6767" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6769" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6771" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="6773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6774" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6776" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6778" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6767" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">âˆ‹</a> <a id="6782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="6783" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6785" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As usual, we have the empty environment, and we can extend an
environment.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="âˆ…&#39;"></a><a id="6892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6892" class="Function">âˆ…&#39;</a> <a id="6895" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6905" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">âˆ…</a>

<a id="_,&#39;_"></a><a id="6914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6914" class="Function Operator">_,&#39;_</a> <a id="6919" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6921" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="6923" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6924" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="6925" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6927" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6924" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6939" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="6946" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6948" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6956" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6924" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="6962" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6979" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6980" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6980" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="6982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6914" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="6985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6985" class="Bound">c</a><a id="6986" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6988" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="6991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6991" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6992" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6994" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6980" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="6998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6991" class="Bound">x</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The following is the big-step semantics for call-by-name evaluation,
which we describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7120" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_âŠ¢_â‡“_"></a><a id="7125" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7125" class="Datatype Operator">_âŠ¢_â‡“_</a> <a id="7131" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7133" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="7135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7135" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="7136" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7138" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="7148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7135" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="7150" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7152" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7135" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="7155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="7157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="7158" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7160" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7167" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7169" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7173" class="Keyword">where</a>

       <a id="7508" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7437" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="7512" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7468" class="Bound">Î´</a> <a id="7540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link          <a id="7570" class="Comment">----------------------------------------------------</a>
       <a id="7630" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7437" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="7634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7125" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="7636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7452" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="7638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Â·</a> <a id="7640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7454" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7125" class="Datatype Operator">â‡“</a> <a id="7644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7498" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* The `â‡“-var` rule evaluates a variable by finding the associated
  closure in the environment and then evaluating the closure.

* The `â‡“-lam` rule turns a lambda abstraction into a closure
  by packaging it up with its environment.

* The `â‡“-app` rule performs function application by first evaluating
  the term `L` in operator position. If that produces a closure containing
  a lambda abstraction `Æ› N`, then we evaluate the body `N` in an
  environment extended with the argument `M`. Note that `M` is not
  evaluated in rule `â‡“-app` because this is call-by-name and not
  call-by-value.

If the big-step semantics says that a term `M` evaluates to both `c` and
`c'`, then `c` and `c'` are identical. In other words, the big-step relation
is a partial function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="â‡“-determ"></a><a id="8439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8439" class="Function">â‡“-determ</a> <a id="8448" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8450" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="8452" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8452" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="8453" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8455" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="8457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="8467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8452" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="8468" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8470" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8474" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8452" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="8476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="8478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="8479" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8481" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8483" class="Bound">c&#39;</a> <a id="8486" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="8492" class="Symbol">}</a>

## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation `ğ•` is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction, i.e., in weak-head normal
form (WHNF). The relation ğ”¼ is for any closure. Roughly speaking,
`ğ”¼ v c` will hold if, when `v` is greater than a function value, `c` evaluates
to a closure `c'` in WHNF and `ğ• v c'`. Regarding `ğ• v c`, it will hold when
`c` is in WHNF, and if `v` is a function, the body of `c` evaluates
according to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ğ•"></a><a id="9279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9279" class="Function">ğ•</a> <a id="9281" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="9289" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9291" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="9296" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9298" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="ğ”¼"></a><a id="9302" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9302" class="Function">ğ”¼</a> <a id="9304" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="9312" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6694" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="9319" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9321" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We define `ğ•` as a function from values and closures to `Set` and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with `ğ”¼` in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then `ğ•` is false (`Bot`). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define `ğ•` by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Æ›</a> <a id="10003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9982" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10004" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9985" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="10007" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10009" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">Ã—</a> <a id="10011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9279" class="Function">ğ•</a> <a id="10013" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9970" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10015" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6713" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10021" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Æ›</a> <a id="10024" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9982" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10025" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9985" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="10028" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* If the value is `âŠ¥`, then the result is true (`âŠ¤`).

* If the value is a join (u âŠ” v), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of ğ• is true for both u and v.

* The important case is for a function value `v â†¦ w` and closure
  `clos (Æ› N) Î³`. Given any closure `c` such that `ğ”¼ v c`, if `w` is
  greater than a function, then `N` evaluates (with `Î³` extended with `c`)
  to some closure `c'` and we have `ğ• w c'`.


The definition of `ğ”¼` is straightforward. If `v` is a greater than a
function, then `M` evaluates to a closure related to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9302" class="Function">ğ”¼</a> <a id="10606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10616" class="Bound">Î³&#39;</a><a id="10618" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10620" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10622" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10633" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="10635" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Î£[</a> <a id="10638" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10638" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the main lemma is by induction on `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). So we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, `ğ”¾`
relates `Î³` to `Î³'` if the corresponding values and closures are related
by `ğ”¼`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ğ”¾"></a><a id="11046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11046" class="Function">ğ”¾</a> <a id="11048" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11050" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="11052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11052" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="11053" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11055" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11057" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="11061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11052" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11063" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6664" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="11073" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11052" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11075" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11077" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

We need a few properties of the `ğ•` and `ğ”¼` relations.  The first is that
a closure in the `ğ•` relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11498" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="11503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11503" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="11508" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11510" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="11512" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11513" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11513" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11515" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11515" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11516" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11518" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11520" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11513" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="11524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11515" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11526" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11528" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="11532" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.Æ›_"></a><a id="11540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11540" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Æ›_</a> <a id="11543" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11545" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="11547" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11548" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11548" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="11549" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11551" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11552" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="11554" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11548" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a> <a id="11562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="11564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="11565" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="11572" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11503" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="11579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Æ›</a> <a id="11582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11552" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11583" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

Next we have an introduction rule for `ğ•` that mimics the `âŠ”-intro`
rule. If both `u` and `v` are related to a closure `c`, then their join is
too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ğ•âŠ”-intro"></a><a id="11992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11992" class="Function">ğ•âŠ”-intro</a> <a id="12001" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12003" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="12005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12005" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="12007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12007" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="12009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12009" class="Bound">v</a><a id="12010" class="Symbol">}</a>

In a moment we prove that `ğ•` is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if `ğ• v c` and `v' âŠ‘ v`, then `ğ• v' c`.
This property, named `ğ•-sub`, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the `sub` rule.

To prove `ğ•-sub`, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to `âŠ¥`. In such cases, `ğ• v (clos (Æ› N) Î³')` is trivially true.

The proofs of `ğ•-sub` and `ğ”¼-sub` are intertwined.

We prove `ğ•-sub` by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
`v' âŠ‘ v`. We describe each case below.

<a id="14995" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="14999" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15001" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚</a> <a id="15006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15006" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="15010" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15012" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">âŠ¥-elim</a> <a id="15019" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15020" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="15034" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15006" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="15038" class="Bound">naf2</a><a id="15042" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15044" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="15048" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15050" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚‚</a> <a id="15055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15055" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="15059" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15061" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">âŠ¥-elim</a> <a id="15068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15069" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="15083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15055" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="15087" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="15091" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `BotâŠ‘`. We immediately have `ğ• âŠ¥ (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `ConjLâŠ‘`.

        vâ‚' âŠ‘ v     vâ‚‚' âŠ‘ v
        -------------------
        (vâ‚' âŠ” vâ‚‚') âŠ‘ v

  The induction hypotheses gives us `ğ• vâ‚' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`
  and `ğ• vâ‚‚' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`, which is all we need for this case. 

* Case `ConjR1âŠ‘`.

        v' âŠ‘ vâ‚
        -------------
        v' âŠ‘ (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)

  The induction hypothesis gives us `ğ• v' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `ConjR2âŠ‘`.

        v' âŠ‘ vâ‚‚
        -------------
        v' âŠ‘ (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us `ğ• v' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `TransâŠ‘`.

        v' âŠ‘ vâ‚‚   vâ‚‚ âŠ‘ v
        -----------------
             v' âŠ‘ v

  The induction hypothesis for `vâ‚‚ âŠ‘ v` gives us
  `ğ• vâ‚‚ (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  for `v' âŠ‘ vâ‚‚` to conclude that `ğ• v' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `DistâŠ‘`. This case  is the most difficult. We have

        ğ• (v â†¦ w) (clos (Æ› N) Î³)
        ğ• (v â†¦ w') (clos (Æ› N) Î³)

  and need to show that 

        ğ• (v â†¦ (w âŠ” w')) (clos (Æ› N) Î³)
  
  Let `c` be an arbtrary closure such that `ğ”¼ v c`.
  Assume `w âŠ” w'` is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both `w` and `w'`
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma `AboveFun-âŠ”`,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.
  
  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    `Î³ âŠ¢ N â‡“ clos L Î´` and `ğ• w (clos L Î´)`.  We also have `Î³ âŠ¢ N â‡“ câ‚ƒ` and
    `ğ• w' câ‚ƒ`.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    `câ‚ƒ â‰¡ clos L Î´`. Also, from `ğ• w (clos L Î´)` we know that `L â‰¡ Æ› N'`
    for some `N'`. We conclude that `ğ• (w âŠ” w') (clos (Æ› N') Î´)`.

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say `AboveFun w` and `Â¬ AboveFun w'`. Then from
    `ğ• (v â†¦ w) (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`
    we have `Î³ âŠ¢ N â‡“ clos L Î³â‚` and `ğ• w (clos L Î³â‚)`. From this we have
    `L â‰¡ Æ› N'` for some `N'`. Meanwhile, from `Â¬ AboveFun w'` we have
    `ğ• w' (clos L Î³â‚)`. We conclude that
    `ğ• (w âŠ” w') (clos (Æ› N') Î³â‚)`.
    

The proof of `sub-ğ”¼` is direct and explained below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#13152" class="Function">sub-ğ”¼</a> <a id="17224" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17225" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6713" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="17230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17230" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="17232" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17232" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="17233" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17235" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17236" class="Bound">v</a><a id="17237" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17239" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17240" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="17242" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17244" class="Bound">ğ”¼v</a> <a id="17247" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17247" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a> <a id="17252" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17252" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="17260" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="17265" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17244" class="Bound">ğ”¼v</a> <a id="17268" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3831" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ‘</a> <a id="17280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17252" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="17284" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17247" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a><a id="17288" class="Symbol">)</a>

From `AboveFun v'` and `v' âŠ‘ v` we have `AboveFun v`.  Then with `ğ”¼ v c` we
obtain a closure `c` such that `Î³ âŠ¢ M â‡“ c` and `ğ• v c`. We conclude with an
application of `sub-ğ•` with `v' âŠ‘ v` to show `ğ• v' c`.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. More formally, if
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v` and `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'`, then `ğ”¼ v (clos M Î³')`. The proof is by
induction on the derivation of `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v` we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the `var` rule.

    <a id="20264" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="20269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18239" class="Function">â†“â†’ğ”¼</a> <a id="20273" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20210" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="20275" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20277" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20278" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20214" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="20279" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20281" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20282" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20218" class="Bound">Î³&#39;</a><a id="20284" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20223" class="Bound">M</a><a id="20288" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20290" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20231" class="Bound">ğ”¾Î³Î³&#39;</a> <a id="20295" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20248" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="20297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3831" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ‘</a> <a id="20309" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20256" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="20313" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20250" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a><a id="20317" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="20319" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="20323" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="20325" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20327" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20327" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="20329" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20331" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20333" class="Bound">Mâ‡“c</a> <a id="20337" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20339" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20339" class="Bound">ğ•v</a> <a id="20342" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a> <a id="20344" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a> <a id="20346" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="20354" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20327" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="20358" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20360" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20333" class="Bound">Mâ‡“c</a> <a id="20366" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#13100" class="Function">sub-ğ•</a> <a id="20374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20339" class="Bound">ğ•v</a> <a id="20377" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a> <a id="20382" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a> <a id="20384" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `var`. Looking up `x` in `Î³'` yields some closure, `clos M' Î´`,
  and from `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'` we have `ğ”¼ (Î³ x) (clos M' Î´)`. With the premise
  `AboveFun (Î³ x)`, we obtain a closure `c` such that `Î´ âŠ¢ M' â‡“ c`
  and `ğ• (Î³ x) c`. To conclude `Î³' âŠ¢ x â‡“ c` via `â‡“-var`, we 
  need `Î³' x â‰¡ clos M' Î´`, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the `kth-x` lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case `â†¦-elim`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ L Â· M â†“ v`.
  The induction hypothesis for `Î³ âŠ¢ L â†“ vâ‚ â†¦ v`
  gives us `Î³' âŠ¢ L â‡“ clos L' Î´` and `ğ• v (clos L' Î´)`.
  Of course, `L' â‰¡ Æ› N` for some `N`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚`,
  we have `ğ”¼ vâ‚ (clos M Î³')`.
  Together with the premise `AboveFun v` and `ğ• v (clos L' Î´)`,
  we obtain a closure `c'` such that `Î´ âŠ¢ N â‡“ c'` and `ğ• v c'`.
  We conclude that `Î³' âŠ¢ L Â· M â‡“ c'` by rule `â‡“-app`.

* Case `â†¦-intro`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ Æ› N â†“ v â†¦ w`.
  We immediately have `Î³' âŠ¢ Æ› M â‡“ clos (Æ› M) Î³'` by rule `â‡“-lam`.
  But we also need to prove `ğ• (v â†¦ w) (clos (Æ› N) Î³')`.
  Let `c` by an arbitrary closure such that `ğ”¼ v c`.
  Suppose `v'` is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that `Î³' , c âŠ¢ N â‡“ c'` and `ğ• v' c'` for some `c'`.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for `Î³ , v âŠ¢ N â†“ v'`
  but we must first show that `ğ”¾ (Î³ , v) (Î³' , c)`. We prove
  that by the lemma `ğ”¾-ext`, using facts `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'` and `ğ”¼ v c`.

* Case `âŠ¥-intro`. We have the premise `AboveFun âŠ¥`, but that's impossible.

* Case `âŠ”-intro`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)` and `AboveFun (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)`
  and need to show `Î³' âŠ¢ M â†“ c` and `ğ• (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚) c` for some `c`.
  Again, by `AboveFun-âŠ”`, at least one of `vâ‚` or `vâ‚‚` is greater than
  a function.

  * Suppose both `vâ‚` and `vâ‚‚` are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚` and `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚‚`
    we have `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ câ‚`, `ğ• vâ‚ câ‚`, `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ câ‚‚`, and `ğ• vâ‚‚ câ‚‚`
    for some `câ‚` and `câ‚‚`. Because `â‡“` is deterministic, we have `câ‚‚ â‰¡ câ‚`.
    Then by `ğ•âŠ”-intro` we conclude that `ğ• (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚) câ‚`.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose `vâ‚` is greater than a function
    value but `vâ‚‚` is not.  By the induction hypotheses for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚`,
    and using `ğ•â†’WHNF`, we have `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚`
    and `ğ• vâ‚ (clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚)`.
    Then because `vâ‚‚` is not greater than a function, we also have
    `ğ• vâ‚‚ (clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚)`. We conclude that `ğ• (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚) (clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚)`.
    
* Case `sub`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, `v' âŠ‘ v`, and `AboveFun v'`.
  We need to show that `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c` and `ğ• v' c` for some `c`.
  We have `AboveFun v` by `AboveFun-âŠ‘`,
  so the induction hypothesis for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v` gives us a closure `c`
  such that `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c` and `ğ• v c`. We conclude that `ğ• v' c` by `sub-ğ•`.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

The adequacy property is a corollary of the main lemma.
We have `âˆ… âŠ¢ Æ› N â†“ âŠ¥ â†¦ âŠ¥`, so `â„° M â‰ƒ â„° (Æ› N)`
gives us `âˆ… âŠ¢ M â†“ âŠ¥ â†¦ âŠ¥`. Then the main lemma gives us
`âˆ… âŠ¢ M â‡“ c` for some `c`.
